Opposition to the Restoration of the Zhalan Coal Mine 62

Restoration Must Wait Until Next Year. Harbin Correspondence, 4th. Regarding the restoration of the Zhalanor coal mine, the board of directors of the Chinese Eastern Railway, jointly instructed the Railway Bureau, to expedite the matter. The Railway Bureau, after receiving the order, delayed its implementation and recently submitted a response to the board of directors stating that there were various difficulties in restoring the mine and that it would not be possible until next year. The board of directors is currently treating this as an outstanding issue that must await the return of Mo Dehui for a formal meeting to resolve. The general contents of the Russian Bureau's original report are as follows: (The work of restoring operations, which began in January of this year, involved extracting and transporting new coal from trenches. The pre-prepared coal reserve of 20,000 tons was completed on May 15th of this year. During the work period, the remaining paving, property, buildings, and technical documents and mining plans in the mining area were examined for research material. Most importantly, mining in the tunnels is not necessary and has very little benefit. It is not because the No. 9 coal tunnel was flooded. If underground work is to be restored, all equipment will not only take time but also cost money, which is equivalent to reopening a new tunnel. It is better to work from open trenches, which is more convenient for transportation. For future underground work, new coal tunnels will have to be opened. Because this involves large sums of money, it is better to mine from open coal trenches. Last year's experiment with coal mined from open coal trenches was quite suitable. As for the planning and restoration work funds, the coal mining period and the coal produced must be thoroughly assessed. For now, only the No. 2 coal mining area of the new coal tunnel is delineated, divided into two sections. The first section is estimated to contain about 700,000 tons of mineable coal, and the second section is estimated to contain about 2 million tons of reserve coal. These estimated quantities are based on reports from the mine's technical personnel and have no accurate data for reference. After the mine was burned, all the boundaries of coal production, the edges of the coal area, the calculation of the amount of coal mined, and the coal quality of each area were completely lost, with no records available. If implemented based on speculation, the water in each flooded coal area must be treated first. Before work can begin, a power plant must be built and pumps purchased, requiring approximately 250,000 rubles. In addition to the cost of laying track and removing soil from the open trenches, the cost of the first 64,000 tons of coal mined has exceeded 919,000 rubles. In summary, the Railway Bureau should allocate this huge sum of money based on the possibility of exploring and mining the coal seams. It must have a clear grasp before allocating the funds for equipment such as power plants and pumps; otherwise, there may be changes that contradict the plan. Furthermore, the area of the coalfield and the thickness of the coal seams should be thoroughly reviewed. Therefore, the Railway Bureau intends to handle the following plan: (1) A report on all the costs of mining approximately 20,000 tons of coal from the open trench will be submitted shortly. (2) During the period when the coal mine is not in operation, all vacant houses will be preserved, and old and broken parts such as boilers and machines will be dismantled. Technical buildings and other useless items will be inventoried. This work will require 32,000 rubles, with 27,000 yuan for dismantling old machines and 4,000 rubles for preservation, from June to December 1930, a total of seven months. It is also found that all the old machines and materials of the mine are valued at approximately 48,000 rubles. This expense will be listed under the item of the severance of diplomatic relations between China and Russia and will be undertaken to explore and mine the coal blocks in the first and second sections listed above. Exploring the coal seams is costly. Because future coal mining will be based on the planned coal seams, the timing of this work will depend on when the mining beds and all equipment are purchased abroad. It takes several months for such tools to be shipped from abroad. If there are no goods in stock abroad and pre-orders are made, it will take even longer. Based on this, the earliest that exploration and mining of coal seams can be carried out is before July of next year, and it will take until the end of the year to complete. 150 coal mining drills will be needed. After the coal seams have been explored, the amount of reserve coal in the first and second coal areas and its coal quality will be studied based on the exploration data. During the exploration period, attention should be paid to measuring the area of the coal seams and the thickness of the coal seam. If the work of exploring the coal seams is actively carried out, it will not be officially started until the beginning of 1931 at the earliest. In order to conserve public funds, it is planned to finalize the above work and then determine the setting up of a power plant and the installation of pumps. The purchase of this paving must be arranged by the end of the summer of 1931, and water can be pumped in early autumn, because the work procedures are too cumbersome and coal cannot be mined until the end of 1931)." The above is the report of the Russian Bureau Director. According to the document from Hua Yupu, the chief of the materials section of the Railway Bureau, to the Directorate of the Chinese Eastern Railway, it states that all old coal tunnels except for No. 9, which is too severely damaged to be easily restored, can be restored, and underground mining saves labor and money. If, as reported by the Russian Bureau Director, open trenches are opened, new beds are purchased, and new stoves are set up, the statement that excavation will begin next year is also a mere formality. The fact is that it is difficult to handle, so why bother with these extra steps? It is reported that the board of directors has also requested this report for reference at future meetings.

Trial Opens in the Case of Shenyang Postal Workers Transporting Opium 63

Shenyang Correspondence: There were originally three cases of personnel from the Liaoning Postal Administration using postal vehicles to transport opium and narcotics. The first case involved the seizure of opium on a postal vehicle, with the offenders being Ma Cheng, Xu Zhenwu, Chen Xingqiao, and others. The second case involved the discovery of empty bags used for transporting opium, with the offenders being Shen Tianjue, Han Shuren, Zhao Guofeng, and others. The third case involved a contract to sell opium that was reported, with the offenders being Du Shichang, Zhang Fengchi, Xu Jingyi, and others. The case of Ma Cheng and others has already been legally sentenced by the local court. The cases of Shen Tianjue and Du Shichang were also opened for trial yesterday by Tang Yinfen, the presiding judge of the criminal court of the local court. As a result, since evidence still needs to be investigated, the defendants were remanded in custody pending a scheduled retrial. The following is a summary of the discovery and interrogation of the two cases:

Shen Tianjue Case: Shen Tianjue was the director of the second branch of the South Manchuria Station. Han Shuren and Zhao Guofeng were bag transfer personnel. The branch has always been a bag transfer point and does not send out postal bags. Shen and other staff who did not know the details used the convenience of mail not being inspected to transport opium from Rehe, Changchun, and Harbin to sell in this port for profit. On February 4, twenty-five postal bags sent from Harbin to Beiping arrived at the South Manchuria Station, and the empty bags were loaded inside. The person in charge was negligent and forgot to take them out. Shen Tianjue urgently telegraphed the Tianjin Bureau to receive the postal bags. The Tianjin Bureau found a dozen empty bags in the postal bags, which were bags used for transporting opium, and could not return them, so they packed them into other bags and transported them back for reuse. Unexpectedly, they were found by the bureau. According to Shen Tianjue's statement on the same day, he had been working at the bureau for more than three years, and the opium transportation was purely done by the bag transfer personnel, and he knew nothing about it. It was only when the postal bags were sent wrong that Zhao Guofeng and Han Shuren reported to him. He was afraid of being suspected and reported to the Deputy Postmaster and later reported to the General Bureau. He also stated that the escaped Yan Zian had no relatives or friends with him, and he did not let him go. Zhao Guofeng stated that he did not know that the postal bags were sent wrong that day, because the person in charge of the bags was Yan Zian, and he was responsible for inspection and receipt, so he could not be held responsible.

Du Shichang Case: Du Shichang and Zhang Fengchi both received and sent mail at the post office outside the Daxi Bianmen. Xu Jingyi was in the receiving and dispatching office of the Yingkou Post Office. The three of them used the opportunity that mail was not inspected and had a contract to transport opium, with a total of seven articles, all of which were transportation methods. The contract was exposed in 1927, and the former Postmaster questioned them but could not find any loopholes. At the end of December of the same year, someone sent an anonymous letter in English to the Postmaster, and Du Shichang was detained at the former Commercial Bureau Police Station. After a joint investigation by the Post Office and the Police Bureau, no secrets were obtained. The Post Office then leniently transferred Du Shichang and others to the Sipingjie Post Office to work. This year, due to the involvement in the Ma case, Du and others were summoned again. Du only admitted that the contract was for transporting fruits and vegetables, but looking at the wording, such as the fourth article, which states that the goods transported each time must be packed in bags, with the weight clearly marked and sealed with lead. If the weight is insufficient or the lead seal is broken, it will be returned immediately; otherwise, it will be considered complete. This proves that it was indeed a contract to transport opium. According to Du Shichang's statement on the same day, in April 1927, Hou Yaohuan in Changchun was related to his colleague Lu Shuyou and said that goods in Fengtian were very cheap and that each person could return to Changchun with a capital of 200 yuan to make a profit. Lu Shuyou, Hou Yaohuan, Du Shichang, Zhang Fengchi, and Xu Jingyi cooperated. Later, the business failed, and someone sent a black letter to the General Bureau in English, which must have been written by someone inside the bureau, or they may have seen the contract language and thought it was similar to an opium transportation contract, so they took this action. It should be known that as a postal worker, I can absolutely not transport opium. If there was opium transportation, the General Bureau would have sent someone to investigate long ago and would not have delayed it until today. Zhang Fengchi stated that the goods to be sold in the contract were vegetables, and he was the representative in charge of the contract, which was written by Du Shichang, and he did not know about it. Xu Jingyi stated that he had been working at the post office for nine years and one month. This contract was for transporting fresh goods, and he signed his name on it. The contract was signed by Du Shichang, and he had never seen it before (June 6th).

Wuhu Quick Dispatch 64

Suddenly, 400 to 500 bandits were discovered in the northwest of Lujiang County. Representatives from all sectors in the local area have specially come to Wuhu to request the garrison regiment stationed in Wuhu to send troops to suppress them and have petitioned the ten-county joint defense office to take measures to prevent and stop them.

The Price Stabilization Committee held a meeting at the General Chamber of Commerce this afternoon. Municipal Director Shao Yizhou, County Magistrate Sun Gongming, Municipal Public Security Bureau Chief, and others attended. They resolved to purchase 20,000 piculs of foreign rice from Shanghai to supplement the people's food supply. In the future, rice sales would be limited to 100 piculs per day, and the price would be raised to 44 copper coins per liter. Furthermore, the three rice mills of Shihuangyuan, Guangbao, Tongxing, and Hunchangyuan were found to be secretly transporting rice out of Wuhu, which was intended to supplement the people's food supply in Wuhu, causing panic among the people. It was decided to immediately seal off the three rice mills and fine them for the loss of 10,000 piculs of flat-priced rice that had already been sold. Additionally, 180 piculs of rice stored in Hunchangyuan were confiscated and the owners of the rice mills were detained and sent to the Public Security Bureau. The Provincial Chamber of Commerce Federation recently stated that the bandit situation in various counties is very serious, and the Anhui province has very few stationed troops. The Wuhu garrison regiment, led by Lu Xueshu, has made great efforts to suppress bandits and has maintained strict discipline. A telegram was specially sent to the Commander-in-Chief and the Nanjing Garrison Commander Gu Zhenglun, requesting permission to allow Lu's regiment to be stationed in Anhui permanently to maintain local order (10th). Local Communication.

Songjiang 65

Long-distance Telephone Rate Reduction: The Construction Bureau announced that since the opening of the long-distance telephone service from Songjiang to Tinglin and Hougang, the fees have been too high, and the public has not been enthusiastic about using it. In order to develop business, it is announced that all long-distance calls will be reduced by five cents, effective from the 11th. County Government Follow-up: Kidnapping Bandits. The kidnapper, Pan Jingqing, a former petty bailiff in Xiaozhengdi, has repeatedly confessed in interrogation. After exposing the chief culprit Zhan, five more accomplices, including Zhu Zilong from Wujingshan, were captured. The county government specifically continued to interrogate the Pan bandit today (11th). He still gave many evasive answers and denied knowing the arrested kidnappers Liu Xiaomei and others, only admitting to hiding a box gun. He denied knowing anything about the circumstances of other local bandits using weapons to rob and provide relief to bandits. It is reported that further interrogations will be conducted in the evening, and a meeting to clear the countryside will be convened on schedule. In this county, robberies have been frequent, and those in rural areas with some wealth have moved to Songjiang to avoid disaster. The county government previously received instructions from higher authorities to organize a countryside clearing bureau to pacify the area. The county government has scheduled the 17th to convene a meeting of various agencies and impartial gentry to discuss organizational methods. It is reported that a countryside clearing general bureau will be established in the county seat, and sub-bureaus will be established in each district.

Suzhou 66

Chen Yiyi's Sentencing Issue: Chen Yiyi, the former Mexican consul, was sentenced by the Jiangning District Court to one year and two months in prison for fraud in connection with the falsification of passports. The charge of falsifying passports was not established. Chen appealed to the High Court, and the trial ended with the fraud charge being dropped and the charge of falsifying passports being upheld, with a sentence of one year and two months in prison. Chen again refused to accept the verdict and has filed another appeal with the Supreme Court. Suddenly, he was involved in a bribery case, and the Jiangning District Court withdrew the case for retrial. The trial ended with a sentence of six months in prison. After the verdict was delivered, Chen accepted the bribery charge without further appeal because the previous case had not yet concluded. However, he claimed that there was an error in the number of days of the sentence and submitted a written statement of reasons to the High Court. Yesterday (10th) afternoon, the High Court Procuratorate sent Prosecutor Sun Xiyan to open a hearing to investigate and calculate the number of days of detention. Jiangdu County Magistrate Accused: Jiangdu County Magistrate Chen Zhao was accused by local figures Xie Jie and others of dereliction of duty due to unfair handling of cases. They submitted a petition to the Procuratorate of the High Court requesting that personnel be dispatched to conduct a thorough investigation. After receiving the petition, the High Court Procuratorate issued an order yesterday (11th) to the Jiangdu County Court Prosecutor to investigate whether the allegations in the case were true and then review it. Third Branch Prison Chief Replaced: Since the Jiangsu Third Branch Prison on Simaqian Street has experienced repeated prison riots, the prison chief and detention center director, Shao Runfen, submitted a resignation request due to the difficulty in handling affairs. High Court President Lin has approved the request and reassigned Ding Lei, the former chief of the county Public Security Bureau Inspectorate, to succeed him. After receiving the appointment, Ding arrived at the post yesterday to assume his duties. Old Copper Coin Factory to Be Rebuilt as Branch Prison: The High Court decided to rebuild the old copper coin factory as a branch prison and sent a letter to the county government yesterday (11th) to investigate the history of the factory's buildings and land. County Magistrate Huang approved the letter and immediately forwarded it to the Construction Bureau for handling.

Fengxian 67

Refugees Causing Disturbances in Rural Areas: In the past two days, a large number of refugees, six to seven hundred people, arrived in the western countryside of this county. Although the Public Security Bureaus of various places dispatched police to suppress them, they caused disturbances wherever they went, and their actions were strange and unusual theft cases occurred. For example, in the 13th district, the Xu family was robbed of decorations and money, and in the 5th district, the Hu residence was robbed of hidden items. The doors and windows were not opened, and the chests and cages were intact. No one knows how they entered. Second Agricultural Education Center Established: The Second Farmers' Education Center of this county has been established. The Education Bureau originally appointed the Preparatory Committee member Qu to serve as the director, but before the announcement could be made, Qu suddenly fell ill and died, preventing the center from opening on schedule. It is now learned that the Education Bureau has reassigned Pei Mian, a graduate of the People's College, to succeed him.

Wuxi 68

Water Police District Captures Notorious Robbers: Mao Mujun, the commander of the Second District of the Wuxi Water Provincial Public Security Team, recently dispatched detectives Zhou Yi and Huang Zhifang to capture two notorious robbers, Zhang Daoyin and Zhang Daochang, at 17 Xia Street, Guangfu Town, Suzhou. They were escorted to Wuxi by train yesterday for interrogation. It is reported that the two criminals were the robbers of the Renchangyuan store in Dongzhu Town, Wuxian County.

Extension of Time Limit for Clearing Accumulated Cases: The county government of this county previously decided that there was a large number of civil and criminal litigation cases, so County Magistrate Sun requested and was approved by the High Court to dispatch a special commissioner, Tang Yiqin, to clear the cases in Wuxi within a time limit of three months. Now, three months have expired, and a total of 170 to 80 cases have been cleared. However, a small portion of the accumulated cases has not yet been adjudicated. Yesterday, County Magistrate Sun submitted a request to the High Court to extend the time limit by one month to allow for complete clearance. Robbery Case Solved, Thieves Escorted Back to Wuxi: Xue Furui, the captain of the detective team of the Public Security Bureau of this county, reported the day before yesterday that informants Wang Bingsheng and others had reported that the leaders of the fugitives who robbed the Bashi Bridge West, Jiaoshan, and Yuxiang Bridge, Zhu Boqing, Tao Jingui, Xu Yibao, and Xu Gengsheng, had recently been surrounded and captured by the Jiangyin County Changshou Township Security. Captain Xue immediately reported to Chief Huang and forwarded the report to County Magistrate Sun of the County Government. County Magistrate Sun immediately prepared a document and ordered Captain Xue to dispatch detectives Dai Shouquan and Chen Erbo to escort the captives back to Cheng. They were escorted to Wuxi and handed over to the Public Security Bureau yesterday morning. In the afternoon, Section Chief Qian opened a court session to interrogate them. All the criminals confessed to the robbery without denying it. After the interrogation, a document was prepared to send them to the county for interrogation and handling.

Changzhou 69

The Wu Yi County government organized a joint defense office and convened a joint military-police-militia defense meeting at 3 PM on the 10th. Over ten representatives from the military, police, business community, and various government agencies attended. County Magistrate Wu chaired the meeting and the following resolutions were passed: (1) The location of the joint defense office will be temporarily set at Chongfa Temple. (2) The commander of the engineering corps was appointed as the director of the office, with the battalion commander of the first Gendarmerie Battalion and the county magistrate as deputy directors. (3) The director would appoint personnel to the office, with each of the seven agencies—the corps headquarters, the Gendarmerie Battalion, the county government, the county party headquarters, the Public Security Bureau, the water police, and the business community—each assigning one person to serve as an officer. (4) A chief detective and four detectives would be appointed and employed after testing by the director and deputy directors. (5) The budget was temporarily set at 150 yuan, and the office affairs meeting would decide how to allocate it. Change of the Fourth District Head: After Liu Baorun, the head of the fourth district of Wu Yi County, left office, the county government assigned Xie Huigong to take over. Recently, the county government received an order from the Civil Affairs Department approving Cheng Foyu to act as the acting head. County Magistrate Wu, upon receiving the order on the 10th, instructed Cheng Foyu to take office and report the details of the handover and reception in accordance with the regulations.

Nantong 70

Provincial Police Squad Goes to Hualong Town to Suppress Bandits: Banditry in the eastern townships of Tongyi is rampant. On the night of the 8th, a group of seven or eight hundred bandits gathered in Hualong Town. The Jiangbei Bandit Suppression Headquarters dispatched the fourth brigade leader of the provincial police, Yu Shimei, to lead his troops and join the special task force to rush to the area. They launched an attack at dawn on the 9th, and after fighting until about 9 o'clock, the bandits suffered heavy casualties and fled to the northeast and east. In this battle, over two hundred bandits were killed and the spoils included one submachine gun, over ten Mauser pistols, and thirty-five Russian-made rifles. These Russian rifles were the ones previously looted from the county police squad. The thirteenth platoon of the provincial police squad suffered injuries to one squad leader and four police officers, who were sent to the Tongcheng Hospital for treatment on the 10th. The pursuit of the fleeing bandits is underway. Convening of a District Head Meeting: The county government convened a meeting of all district heads of the county on the 10th, chaired by Zhang Dong, to discuss and resolve the following important matters: (1) Implement training for township heads and deputies. (2) The principle of the security group is to draw personnel, and in special circumstances, self-employment of responsible substitutes is permitted. (3) Urge the payment of village clearing funds. (4) Security group donations will be borne by wealthy businesses in each district. The rampant situation of the communist bandits in the eastern part of the county: After the communist bandits looted the eastern district, all public officials fled. Recently, a group of over three hundred bandits have been causing trouble in the town, posting reactionary slogans along the streets and firing guns to demonstrate their power. All businesses in the city are unable to open, creating a somber atmosphere as the year ends.

Jiangyin 71

Financial Bureau Seeks to Borrow Police Salary Funds: Because the local expenses for April have not yet been cleared, except for the public security bureau police salaries are urgent and unavoidable, after consultation, the Finance Bureau was asked to borrow nine thousand silver dollars from Qianzhuang to maintain it. This loan will be deducted from the county surtax items that have not yet been collected. Two Rape Cases Occurred in Urban and Rural Areas: Hu Jin'ao, a tenant of Zhang Houji in the north of the city who used to be a tea servant, married a woman named Qin, who worked in a yarn factory and had a son in his teens. He engaged Lu Yuemei from Anquan Village as his wife. At the age of eleven, he brought back the child bride. Recently (the 9th), while dumping a chamber pot in the backyard, she was molested by Feng Zenglin, the supervisor of Hongchang distillery. The tenant saw her and told her aunt, who took her to the first police station for interrogation. Yuemei confessed that she had been raped by Feng four times, etc. On the 10th, she was transferred to the General Bureau for interrogation and then transferred to the county government to be questioned on the 11th. Furthermore, Wang Yingdi (17 years old), the younger sister of Zhao Genda from Houmei Township, accused Shao Heshang and Fan Shunda of the same village of luring and raping her, and abducting her to Wu Fugen's house in Jiang City, where she stayed for four nights. She was sent to the Public Security Bureau for questioning on the 10th and transferred to the county government for questioning. As a result, the confessions of each party were different. The court ordered Wang Yingdi to be sent to the Gospel Hospital for examination to determine whether she was a virgin before further verification.

Jingjiang 72

Bandit Alarm Occurs in Yaojia Ao: Yao Xiaochun and Yao Tingju, brothers and nephews living in the same house in Yaojia Ao, eastern township, were transplanting seedlings on the night of the 7th when a group of bandits armed with military weapons suddenly broke into the house. Xiaochun and his nephew's wife were arrested and beaten. All the cash, two gold rings, and fifty silver dollars in the house were robbed, with the total loss of about six hundred yuan, including clothing. The documents were found by the bandits. After many pleas and additional silver, they were released. A stack of wheat from their neighbor Yao Yixiao was also burned by the bandits. The capture of the bandit party secretary on June 8, the bandit party held a meeting at Jijiashi Shuidongtang, plotting wrongdoing. This was detected by the local security regiment, who went to suppress them, but the bandits learned of it and fled in advance, so only the secretary Guo Litang was captured. The name has now been sent to the county for interrogation.

Zhenjiang 73

Civil Affairs Department Reappoints Two County Public Security Bureau Chiefs: Yesterday, the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province appointed Zou Wusan as the chief of the Danyang County Public Security Bureau and Fang Ruzhou as the chief of the Gaochun County Public Security Bureau and concurrently the captain of the police brigade. Bandits from Gaozi Fled to Jurong: A group of bandits were discovered in Gaozi Dongchang Street. Xu Yuyin, the inspector general of the Public Security Bureau, and Wang Yupei, the brigade commander, led the security second and third companies to pursue them. It is reported that the team set off on the evening of the 9th and searched overnight in Shima Temple Wei Port and other places without finding any trace of the bandits. The next morning, gunshots were heard from the cave. The inspector general led the team to attack. After an hour, the bandits were defeated and fled to Maoshan in Jurong. The team only captured three suspects and returned to the town on the evening of the 10th. According to visitors from Gaozi, the bandits first robbed many houses when they entered the village, and then occupied the area for a day. They entered the village at 11:00 PM and did not leave until 6:00 PM the next afternoon. Before leaving, they burned down two buildings and left a letter agreeing to come back for three or four days. The village is now actively preparing and deploying defenses, and has requested the garrison to pay attention to prevent the bandits from returning. Tea Room Worker Rapes Female Guest: Room 17 of the Yuelai Hotel in Xiaomatou was occupied by a female guest named Zhou Han. In the middle of the night, Wu Baozhi, a tea room worker, climbed into the room from the adjacent room through the wall with the intention of raping Ms. Han. Ms. Han refused to comply and screamed for help. Hu Rongxuan, the doorman of the Seventh Branch, heard the sound and notified patrol leader Liu Zhendong, who investigated and learned the details. Both were taken to the bureau for questioning. Wu confessed without hesitation. The patrol officer of the bureau went to the hotel to keep the footprints and handprints in the two rooms for the court to investigate, and Wu Baozhi and others were sent to the court for punishment.

Yangzhou 74

The Water Police Squad Intercepts Major Opium Smugglers: Yesterday (the 9th), the police squad of the fifth district of the Water Public Security Bureau, stationed at the port, discovered thirteen packages of opium (weighing 632 taels) hidden in the suitcases and rattan boxes of passenger Chen Weijia, who was discovered at the port on the 7th. After a preliminary trial by the squad, he was sent to the Jiangdu County Court for interrogation. Memorial Ceremony for Fallen Police Officers: The Zhenwumiao and Qishumiao garrison police squads in the county held a memorial ceremony at the Great Stage at 2 PM on the afternoon of the 10th for police officers Yu Deshui, Zhao Xingcheng, Xu Shangyu, and others who died in the line of duty. The ceremony was attended by all members of the Public Security Bureau police squad and people from all walks of life. There were many wreaths and elegies from various organizations and groups, and more than a thousand representatives and people attended. A Prostitute Commits Suicide by Drowning: Cai Xizi, the 14-year-old sister of singing girl Hua Luyun from No. 15 Dashu Lane in the city, committed suicide by drowning outside Xuningmen yesterday afternoon (the 8th). Yesterday afternoon, the body floated in the river outside Fuyunmen. After being salvaged by people, it was claimed by the household to prepare a coffin for burial. It is indeed tragic.

Jiaxing 75

Conflict Between Militia and Police Occurs in Youchegang: In the afternoon of the 9th, the police station in Youchegang, northern Jiaxing, arrested carpenter Pan, who was holding sparrow tiles in front of the station, and took him to the station for questioning. Pan, fearing punishment, said that the sparrow tiles were borrowed from Dai, the head of the security team. Pan was then released and the tiles were confiscated. Later, it is not known why, but the police officers had a conflict with the security team members Xu Wenyuan, Hu Jiajun, Hu Zhangkui, etc. The three team members Xu, Hu, etc. were stabbed with knives by police officer Li Maosheng. The knife was then seized by Hu Jiajun, and the police officers were also injured. Afterwards, Yuan Guoan, the patrol leader of the police station, and police officers Li Maosheng, Yang Gentang, Miao Peishen, etc. returned to the station and reported the incident to the Tanghui sub-bureau. Wu Haoran, the head of the sub-bureau, prepared a document based on the report and sent the injured police to the court for examination at noon on the 10th. The three injured team members were sent by the head of the team to the Tianning Hospital in Tianning Village for treatment. The hospital diagnosed that Xu Wenyuan had a knife wound on his left thigh, Hu Zhangkui had a knife wound on his thigh, and Hu Jiajun had a knife wound on his left gluteal muscle. On the afternoon of the 10th, the injured also went to the Jiaxing Branch for an injury examination. On the other hand, the security team filed a complaint with the county government to investigate. The police station chief sent a telegram requesting corrections to two errors of the Construction Bureau: There are many errors in the recent facilities of the Jiaxing County Construction Bureau. For example, the demolition of the southern city has been going on for two years. All the surrounding open space and the land around Nanguo have been approved by the former urban district engineering office and the demolition and construction association to separately grade and set prices for uniform marking and sale. However, the county Construction Bureau has not yet issued licenses with the county seal for the land that has been sold, so the buyers dare not build houses. Moreover, the Construction Bureau handles all the steps of local construction, from planning to facilities to completion acceptance. Outsiders dare not criticize the quality of the project. It seems that there is an element of monopoly. Zhou Guoxun, a county resident, has telegraphed the provincial government requesting a thorough review and strict order to the Jiaxing County government to pay attention to the construction.

Jiashan 76

Two Merchant Giants Hold Funerals: It is reported that Mr. Wen Fulin was a giant merchant from Ningbo living in Jiashan. He has been reported in this newspaper for many years. In addition to running Wen Hengyu and various branches, he was able to generously assist public undertakings such as the Ning Shao Guild Hall and the Debt Association without fear of hardship. He was highly respected by his fellow villagers. He passed away on the 7th of last month. Those who heard about it regretted it. It is now scheduled to hold a funeral on the 14th of this month. At that time, there must be a grand occasion with plain cars and white horses. Bandits Attempt to Rob Liantang Town: Yesterday, rumors spread in Liantang Town, Qingpu County, that bandits were gathering in Xiaozheng New Town to rob Liantang. The town got wind of it and was on alert day and night to prevent accidents. The river surface near Xiaozheng has seen increasing incidents of ship robbery, and walking on land is even more dangerous. Fire Injures People: Yesterday afternoon at 4 o'clock in Fangjia, Fengdong Shilou, a fire broke out in the home of farmer Chu Sanhe, destroying seventeen houses and burning to death Chu Qi, Fang Gu, and two oxen and a sheep. Fei Daguan, Gu Jinsheng, Lu Azhao, Xu Sanmao, and other four people were injured in the fire.

Haining 77

Cocoon Donation Bureau Chief Accused of Overcharging: The Haining Cocoon Industry Association accused Qiu Zhenglun, the director of the Haining Cocoon Donation Bureau, of abusing his powers and using administrative penalties such as ordering the Chang'an Silk Factory to suspend work and arbitrarily fining He Tai Cocoon Bank a large sum of money, and even levying the cost of each cocoon package stamp issued by the Finance Department at five cents, creating new loopholes. Recently, it was found that cocoons transported and sold within the territory were not exempted from the donations of the three provincial public offices as in the past. His methods of collecting money can be described as meticulous. It is found that there are a total of 109 cocoon firms in Haining this year, and the dry cocoons sold to Shuangshan and Chang'an silk factories are not in the minority, and those sold to silk factories in Hangzhou, Jiaxing, and Huzhou also have. Although the donations of the three provincial public offices are only one angle for every hundred catties of cocoon, the total amount has reached several hundred yuan. Such private malpractice violates the party members' oath. A telegram was sent to the Zhejiang Provincial Government requesting that the Director of the Bureau be strictly ordered to return the overcharged donations of the three provincial public offices for cocoons transported and sold within the territory to the cocoon firms in order to comply with the practice and prevent embezzlement.

Ningbo 78

Butcher Shop Strike Has Turned For The Better: The Ningbo Municipal Government believes that the various facilities for slaughtering pigs and sheep in the butcher shops in the urban area have always been inadequate, so it established the Second Slaughterhouse in July last year, which was completed on the first day of this month. However, a few butcher shops actually resisted and involved all the butcher shops in the city in a unified slaughter strike, which has lasted for nearly a week. It is reported that the Municipal Government, in consideration of the meat industry's business, has decided to convene representatives from each butcher shop at the market at 10:00 AM on the 10th to jointly discuss and eliminate mutual prejudices.

June 12th, 1930 (Third Edition of Shen Bao) Education News

Important News

Liaoning Education Funds 79

This year's total is more than 4.27 million yuan (Shenyang Communication) The funding standards for the various education bureaus in Liaoning Province have now been separately determined by the Department of Education to be six levels: 150,000 yuan for the first level, 120,000 yuan for the second level, 90,000 yuan for the third level, 60,000 yuan for the fourth level, 40,000 yuan for the fifth level, and 40,000 yuan for the sixth level. The funding levels described are also determined based on the level of students in each county. Those with more than 600 students are in the first level, those with more than 450 students are in the second level, those with more than 300 students are in the third level, those with more than 200 students are in the fourth level, those with more than 100 students are in the fifth level, and those with more than 100 students are in the sixth level. The table is as follows: County Student Level of Estimated Funding for 1929 Level of Approved Estimated Funding for 1930 Shenyang 8111 125000 9711 Liaoyang 7791 152189 11 Jin County 3533 96062 33 Xinmin 5662 125788 22 Yingkou 2684 80175 44 Jinxi 2264 39904 65 Panshan 1695 38952 65 Yixian 3543 104790 33 Xingcheng 2084 40250 54 Liaozhong 5032 77247 43 Haicheng 6711 119980 32 Gaiping 5502 137250 22 Tieling 4522 113609 33 Kaiyuan 4892 64688 11 Beizhen 3093 70992 43 Suizhong 3123 39474 64 Zhangwu 1095 38340 65 Heishan 3053 52663 54 Dongfeng 3213 152988 12 Xi'an 2674 94764 33 Xifeng 2764 85273 43 Tai'an 2154 32120 64 Hailong 2214 101411 33 Changbai 3061 83896 6 Xinbin 2444 90818 33 Fengcheng 4253 47935 54 Zhuanghe 4912 86582 43 Huinan 7264 111755 Fuxian 4882 67506 43 Xiuyan 3043 60776 43 Fushun 3253 88360 43 Benxi 2774 39251 65 Tonghua 1395 77600 44 Huanren 1395 54673 55 Ji'an 1145 51347 55 Linjiang 8964 44431 55 Andong 2724 48281 54 Kuandian 3113 41536 54 Fusong 3262 110466 Antu 1869 19066 Liuhe 1425 81700 44 Changtu 4483 145510 22 Taonan 1015 73213 44 Huaiku 3783 90485 33 Liaoyuan 9465 512955 Kaitong 4162 724966 Tao'an 4263 485866 Anguang 3663 393966 Tuquan 3962 295566 Zhendong 4061 762766 Lishu 2744 15122313 Huaide 3073 10459033 Kangping 1905 5811255 Shuangshan 4461 980466 Zhanyu 3961 1291166 Tongliao 1085 7880444 Qingyuan 1365 4679055 Jinchuan 4062 311866 The above table is based on the average number of student levels and the amount of education funding for the 18th year in the entire territory in the first quarter of the 19th year. Those whose academic level is two levels higher than the funding level will be raised one level, and those who are four levels higher will be raised two levels. Conversely, those whose academic level is lower than the funding level will also be downgraded accordingly. The downgrading of remote counties should be considered and exempted from (Huanhua).

Ministry of Education Cancels Recruitment by Labor University 80

The Ministry of Education previously sent personnel to inspect the Labor University in conjunction with the Director of the Shanghai Special City Education Bureau, and later invited experts to inspect it, believing that the management was not in compliance. It was recently seen that the school claimed to have contacted the Ministry of Education and advertised for recruitment. The Ministry of Education specially issued a bulletin on the 10th to cancel the recruitment of students by the Labor University, stating that the Ministry has now ordered the Labor University to stop recruiting new students for fear of not being fully informed. It also heard that the Ministry of Education is earnestly rectifying private universities that are not properly managed and will issue another bulletin soon. On the 10th, a reporter saw Minister Jiang talking about the reorganization of the Labor University. The reply meant that the purpose of suspending recruitment was not to stop running the school, but to seek appropriate changes and improvements in the organization and existing students of the university so as not to fail the country's original intention of cultivating labor talents. This matter is entirely a matter of organization and not a matter of people, said the Ministry of Education.

Strict Prohibition of Gambling Tools Hidden in Fountain Pens 81

The Ministry of Education, according to the Department of Education of Rehe Province, forwarded a case of gambling tools hidden in imported fountain pens and requested that it be strictly prohibited. The Ministry specially instructed the Departments of Education in each province and city, saying: According to the report of the Department of Education of Rehe Province, the school supervisor of Chaoyang County, Yuan Fenghou, found that a fountain pen with the Sekai trademark of the T·O·Company of Tokyo, Japan, had three bone dice hidden in the spiral cover at the top, which were obviously gambling tools. In addition to ordering the counties and bureaus under its jurisdiction to strictly prohibit the sale, it was transferred for review and approval to order all provinces to strictly prohibit it to prevent harming young people and developing bad habits, etc., and attached the original pen and a paper explaining the drawings to the ministry. It was found that this kind of fountain pen was manufactured with cultural utensils to lead gambling, which is a hindrance to education and should be strictly prohibited. In addition to distributing orders, the original fountain pen structure diagram and a paper explaining the order were copied and sent to you to comply with the prohibition of purchase and use, and to order all subordinates to comply with this order, including copying the original pen diagram and a paper explaining it (omitted).

Chuansha Public Elementary School Opens Two Major Events 82

Lu Rongan, the principal of Chuansha County Public Elementary School, meticulously plans the school's affairs, so it always ranks first in various county competitions. On the morning of the 8th of this month, the school held a separate science experiment competition and a public lecture. Starting at 2 pm, a parents' day was held with many attendees. There were more than 40 experiment and performance programs, and the audience was very satisfied.

Municipal Education Bureau Sets Examination Rules 83

Junior High School: The Municipal Education Bureau has set the following examination rules for junior high school graduates: (1) Examinees must bring a recent four-inch photo of themselves when taking the first party ideology examination. (2) Examinees must take the seats designated by the proctors and must not change them. (3) Examinees must not whisper to each other during the examination. Those who violate this rule will not be allowed to participate in the examination. (4) Examinees must not bring in materials or have someone take the examination for them. Those who violate this rule will not be allowed to participate in the examination. (5) Examinees must not bring any books except for ink boxes and arithmetic tools. (6) Examinees must adhere to the scheduled examination time and must not extend it. (7) Examinees must adhere to all orders from the proctors. (8) Each student will only receive one copy of the examination paper for each subject. (9) Examinees who must temporarily leave the examination hall due to special circumstances must obtain the permission of the proctor. (10) No one other than special Municipal Education Bureau staff, proctors, and examinees may enter the examination hall. (11) These rules will take effect from the date of their promulgation. Elementary School: Seven points of student knowledge for the Elementary School Graduation Examination were set as follows: (1) Examinees must arrive at the venue before the scheduled examination time. (2) After arriving at the venue, examinees should check which room they should take the examination in. (3) Examinees who are more than 20 minutes late will be disqualified from the examination. (4) The name of the school and the name should be written on the floating ticket of the examination paper. The name of the district, the name of the school, and the student number on the examination paper must not be filled in, otherwise the examination paper will be invalid. (5) Examinees must obey the proctor's orders during the examination and must not talk, look around, leave their seats, bring in materials, or copy, otherwise the examination paper will be invalid. (6) Draft paper will be issued by the Bureau and must not be self-prepared. (7) Examinees should leave their seats immediately after handing in their papers.

Ministry of Education Has No Concrete Plan for Promoting Physical Education 95

Zhang Boling requests a stipulation that every elementary school establish a sports field. Minister Jiang believes that the political situation is unstable and that there are no economic resources at this time, but he will strive to promote physical education universally within feasible limits. On the afternoon of the 10th, the reporter met Minister of Education Jiang Menglin at the Ministry. During a brief conversation, they discussed the reasons for China's disastrous defeat at the Far Eastern Games. The gist of the conversation is recorded below: Mr. Zhang Boling, the Chief Representative of China at the previous Far Eastern Games, visited the Ministry to discuss the situation of the Far Eastern Games held in Japan. The conversation was quick. Mr. Zhang suggested that physical education should be made a compulsory subject starting from elementary school, and that necessary equipment for physical education should be stipulated. Every elementary school must have a sports field, etc., which should be implemented uniformly by all schools nationwide through an order from the Ministry of Education. Mr. Zhang's proposition is undoubtedly the best way to promote physical education. However, China is now impoverished and financially strained. It is impossible to fully realize this in a short period of time. Therefore, in my view, the reasons for the failure of Chinese athletes in this Far Eastern Games are numerous, but they are all minor details. The only fundamental reason is the overall political problem in China. Without political stability in the country, nothing can be discussed. In our current situation, reactionary elements are causing disturbances everywhere, disasters are rampant, and the people are impoverished and in extreme distress. The difficulty of making a living for the people leaves no time to promote physical education. Furthermore, the lack of adequate nutrition in ordinary diets, the poor social environment, the lack of medical hygiene, and the weak productivity of the people are all directly and indirectly related to the cultivation of athletes. All these things can only be gradually improved after China's political situation stabilizes as soon as possible. At present, financial resources are stretched thin, and land prices in cities are quite high. Recently, the Ministry of Education planned to buy a piece of land nearby to build housing, which is already proving difficult. The financial capacity of each school to purchase a sports field is even more conceivable. Therefore, to hope that every elementary school is equipped with a sports field, one must first hope that the country's political situation will stabilize as soon as possible and that the social economy will develop as soon as possible. However, as long as I am in office, I will always take an active attitude and strive to promote the universality of physical education training nationwide within the possible range. The day will eventually come when China will avenge its failure in sports. B: Of course, I'll be put in a coffin and buried in the ground, and that's it.

The Youthful Life of Mussolini by Wu Pingzhong 99

The Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, who holds numerous positions, whose words are decrees, whose actions change the world, and who does not hesitate to make enemies of the world to restore Italy's former glory, is regarded by the world with astonishment as a strange character. Some of his youthful life is worth recording, so I note it below: Mussolini came from a poor background. His father was a blacksmith, and he learned the trade from him from a young age. If he made even a slight mistake, his father would not be lenient with his fists. However, Mussolini initially had no resentment and was grateful for his father's strict supervision. At the age of nine, he entered the village elementary school. He was both a student and an apprentice. Although the class divisions between rich and poor students were obvious and teachers inevitably showed prejudice, Mussolini was diligent and cheerful and did not care at all. Later, he transferred to a normal school. At that time, he was highly regarded by teachers and friends, as his literary and oratorical talents had gradually emerged. After graduating, he worked as a teacher in a small school, spending every day from morning to night with dozens of naughty children. Whenever he felt extremely bored, he would concentrate and play a few pieces of violin music to entertain himself. This man, as fierce as a tiger and with a spirit that overwhelms mountains and rivers, has a unique interest in heart-stirring music. Is this not a strange thing? Later, he lost his teaching position and joined an immigration group to seek a living far away. When he arrived in Switzerland, he ran around all day looking for work but could not find any. He was penniless, suffered from hunger and cold, and could not get enough to eat. At night, he slept in parks or broken boat cabins on the lake, and was often driven away and humiliated by the police. His difficult, wandering, and helpless life was probably what tempered his indomitable personality. Mussolini once enlisted in the army and became an Italian infantryman. He also served as the chief writer for newspapers several times, writing articles attacking the government and vigorously advocating patriotism. His sentiments were passionate and deeply moving, but his writing was too sharp and he was repeatedly arrested for being too radical. However, little did people know that the disheveled prisoner of that day would be the prime minister who would later take control of the entire country. Mussolini's heart is devoted to the country, but his ferocity and tyranny have both praise and criticism. It is difficult for us to make a judgment for a while, but his courage and perseverance are truly admirable. Compared to those in our country who are decadent and unmotivated and do not take responsibility for their actions, how far apart is his virtue?

The Big Rats of Jingdezhen · Die · Hua 101

Jingdezhen, located in Jiangxi, is a famous region for porcelain production. Residents there have never paid attention to hygiene. The abundance of rats there is rare in the world. The rats not only jump and run around in broad daylight, but also walk on the streets without any fear. Recently, Jingdezhen has been plagued by rice shortages, and porcelain factories have successively stopped production. The rats have also suffered from food shortages and are becoming increasingly disturbed. A certain porcelain merchant, unable to bear the rat infestation, bought several cats in the hope of suppressing them. Unexpectedly, the cats not only failed to catch the rats, but were instead bitten by them. The owner of the shop, at his wit's end, devised a trap to catch rats in rice jars and caught a large rat more than a foot long, with black fur with a golden hue and teeth as sharp as blades. It weighed more than three pounds. It is said that the owner of the shop, seeing the rampant rats and the ineffectiveness of the cats, will offer a reward for rat-catching devices to eliminate this problem. This is after the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom occupied it as its capital during the mid-Qing Dynasty. It was later destroyed by the Qing army. After the devastation of war, the beautiful prosperity turned to ashes. After nearly a hundred years, its vitality has not been restored. Since the National Government established its capital here, a new atmosphere has emerged. The former palace of weeds and millet now has towering summer houses. The former streets lined with people's houses now have vermilion gates facing each other or have been leveled into Zhongshan Avenue. On the streets of the past, only horse-drawn carriages and chartered cars bumped and galloped. Now, cars are racing in succession. From the perspective of material construction, it has gradually transformed from a dilapidated classical city into a modern city. Also, people in the capital now call Xiushan Park "Blood Flower Park" or "Zhongshan Park," and visiting the imperial tomb or Ming Xiaoling Mausoleum is now called "visiting Zhongshan Mausoleum." The singing girls along the Qinhuai River have been replaced by performing artists, and fortune-tellers have been replaced by document writers. Advertisements for imperialist goods on the walls have also been largely overthrown by revolutionary slogans. Other examples include the transformation of the military governor's office into the National Government, Southeast University into Central University, the police department into the public security bureau, and the magistrate into the county head. All these reflect the new face of revolution. During the two days, I visited the Gulin Temple and the ancient woods and bamboo forests around Qingliang Mountain, admired the new lotus and tender reeds of Mochou Lake, and paddled the small oars and clear waves of Xuanwu Lake, as well as visited the crops of the university's farm and caressed the ancient pines of the Mei Nunnery. Revisiting the old places evoked new feelings. I deeply felt that the green hills, clear waters, abundant grass, and long forests here were full of life, pleasing my ears and eyes and benefiting my mind and spirit.

Travel Notes from Southeast Asia (27) Linghua 103

On the 12th, my feet suffered from dampness. The temple monk turned martial arts master gave me a prescription, and many friends gave me many medicines. I didn't know which to choose, which shows how difficult it is to choose a prescription. Therefore, in the Avatamsaka Sutra, Sudhana's fifty-three visits all say that he has made up his mind but does not know how to practice the Dharma. Regarding the problem of feet suffering from dampness in Southeast Asia, it is also a question for those who come here. The original words vary from person to person, and it is difficult for me to judge. Some told me not to take too many showers, once a day is enough, or said that I must take many showers, or said that the way to take a shower must be to shower from the top and down, and it is best to open your eyes so that people can hear the sound of the water flowing, and you should never take a bath like in China. While showering, you must vigorously rub the heat out of your body, and the most important thing is to wipe your feet dry after the heat flows down to your feet to avoid moisture, which is the cause of the disease. I have read all kinds of things and it is difficult for me to follow them one by one. Or some said that you must take a shower at dawn, so you will not be tired all day, and even if you don't take a shower during the day, it is okay. I used to take a shower at 11 o'clock when I felt hot, but now I take a shower every morning, and the disease really gets better. Maybe it's effective. In short, the climate in Southeast Asia is hot and unsuitable for guests. Those who grow up here don't have to worry, but those who come here must pay attention. The only important thing to resist the heat is to use the coldness of the water to reduce the heat on the body, which is more important than food and drink. Those who come here should pay attention to it. On the 13th, I had a minor illness. I had been paying attention for a long time to the question of the people of Southeast Asia and studying what kind of people the black fruits of black people belong to and where their blackness comes from. I couldn't get the point for a long time. Some said that this is a member of the Indian people called the Ji Neng people or the Ji Ning people, or said that their race is black and born like this, or some people said that it is black from sea bathing, or said that it is black because of applying a kind of oil, or said that their children are not black, or said that they are black because of sea bathing and oil. I thought that the sea is not sure to make people black, why are sea fish scales white and not black. One day, Zhang Xuanjun explained it and said, "Why are you doubting? Chickens have black chickens, red chickens, and white chickens. Horses have black horses, white horses, and yellow horses. Cattle, dogs, pigs, and sheep all have five colors and are born naturally. Why must there be a reason? Aren't people animals with five colors? Why must you test where they come from one by one?" I suddenly realized that I had been studying zoology for a long time, but it was Zhang Jun who revealed that the five races are just like the five-colored animals. Then how can you say that white is good-looking and the rest are not good-looking? How can you say that yellow is superior and black is inferior? Color is equal. It is true equality. Although this is said, even our yellow people are afraid of the blackness of black people. Their color is like molten iron and cannot be washed away. They are really like black chickens, and their bodies are hairy and their skin is not clean. Their curly hair is straight like black ghosts. I often look at them closely. The blackness is like human bones. If I meet them in our country in the middle of the night, no one will doubt that they are people. People will definitely doubt that they are ghosts. No doubt, children and women are really scary. Black people are honest and mostly stay outside the doors of Chinese people, wearing two pieces of cloth to cover their upper and lower bodies. They have nothing else. Those who work for the British are given a standing star by the government. This is the kindness of the ruler. Black people like to wrap their heads and wear floral skirts. The colors are bright in the Malay area, but the colors are lighter in Java. Some young black people also imitate European dress, and white clothes make them even blacker. (The number 27 marked under yesterday's title was a mistake for 26.) There are all kinds of musical instruments, such as organs, pianos, and violins. In addition to musical instruments, there are Go, Chinese chess, and military chess. When playing chess, a blind child and a sighted student were fighting hard. I watched carefully from the side. After a while, all the chariots and horses east of the Honggou were taken by the blind child, and then he killed his Chu commander and won a great victory. It is said that blind people have a calm mind and often win chess games. I think that if you can focus on one thing, you can definitely make progress. The value of blind people playing chess lies in their concentration. Blind people's special skills are amazing. After a while, I suddenly heard the military music and went to the large playground in front of the school building to watch the recreational activities. Men and women sat together and watched around like a wall. The programs included blind children singing party songs and playing military flutes, which were sad and passionate like the cold reed pipes outside the Great Wall. The acrobats stacked pyramids and human mountains quickly and skillfully. The instructor clapped his hands as a signal, but the audience who witnessed the stunt could not applaud for fear of disturbing the blind people's movements, which was also interesting. Heartfelt Warmth (220) Bao Tianxiao 104

Chapter Eleven: Emerald Locks and Pearl Hairpins, a Beauty Returns. Jialiyi, a brothel adorned with red pavilions, a famous courtesan marries into a prominent family. At this time, Ah Jin said from the side, "Second Master Yi, why don't you write a note tomorrow to invite her? There have been very few performances lately, and it's almost the holidays. She even said yesterday that she wanted to treat me to a big meal!" Ah Jin said this, and Ruiyun did not deny it, so it was decided. Zuo Shichen said, "Tomorrow around seven or eight o'clock, I'll write a note at Yizhixiang to invite you." Yizhixiang is very close to Qinghefang, and you pass by there seventeen or eight times every day after your performance, Ruiyun suddenly said. "Don't you invite me. I'll invite you tomorrow," Shichen said. "What's the reason for that?" Ruiyun said, "Then what's the reason for your inviting me?" Shichen said, "Haven't I invited you before? This time, inviting you is just like you're going on a long journey, and I'm here to see you off." Ruiyun said, "I didn't invite you specifically. I've told Ah Jin several times that we should also have a comfortable big meal. I've promised her several times, but the damn performances are always three, four, fourteen, fifty every day. Where do I have the time for that? Now that there are fewer performances, I'm inviting Ah Jin to invite you to be the guest of honor." Shichen quickly agreed, "Okay, okay, I'll be the guest of honor." On this day, the head madam was going back and forth between the front and back rooms, looking like she was very proud of herself. She also wanted to hear what you were talking about. She didn't know whether Ruiyun was happy or worried. As usual, those in the brothel who were getting someone from the madam's hands to marry couldn't get the person's consent. Even if a guest in the brothel wanted someone, they would only discuss it with their fake mother and never seek the person's consent. Therefore, those who made a living in the brothel had no personal freedom at all. Whoever she wants you to marry, you marry. You have no choice but to obey. There is no possibility of resistance. Even if there is someone you are happy to marry, but your fake mother, your owner, refuses to allow it, there is nothing you can do. Under this kind of situation, those poor things that are delicate and graceful cannot be considered a person. They can only be considered a kind of animal, and a kind of animal that is kept and imprisoned. Just like livestock, sometimes they use your strength, and sometimes they sell you out. Until now, this system of selling people is still prevalent, and I don't know how many good daughters have been killed. Someone like Ruiyun is still someone that the head madam usually loves, but this unwritten law that getting someone to marry in the brothel requires the person's consent cannot be broken. She just kept telling Ruiyun how good the Zhang family was, and also said that on that day, I would teach them to use a carriage to pick you up, just like people welcoming a bride. The windows of the carriage should also be covered with red silk. Although you are becoming a concubine, you don't need to have a wedding ceremony, but you have to look good when you go out. Now, which of your girlfriends doesn't envy you? It's just like the moth's own Zhang Lang's brush. The mother is diligent in doing makeup for the daughter. I don't know what will happen in the future, so listen to the next chapter.

Finance 105

Gold Market Resumes Its Ascent 106

Market Fluctuations and Uncertainty Result in a Gain of 4.9 Taels; Transition from Weakness to Peak

Yesterday's gold market was quite chaotic, with sudden and unpredictable changes. Fluctuations of several taels were common and difficult to grasp. Throughout the day, the price difference reached as much as fifteen or sixteen taels, but the overall trend shifted from weakness to a peak. Foreign exchange rates had been rising, but internal conditions improved. Among brokers, transactions involving promissory notes were frequent, with varying demand and supply. However, the market sentiment was uncertain. Firms such as Zhifeng, Yongcheng, Fengyong, and Yong Shengchang, as well as speculators, were generally selling off. Fuchang, Wanxing, and Kunhe, among others, were buying. Early in the day, large transactions pushed the market slightly higher, but the overall trend was flat. Later, major players leaned towards selling, fueled by rumors that Ministers Kong and Song were considering measures to address the gold price surge and silver depreciation, including a proposal to the national government to temporarily suspend operations of the Gold Exchange. This sparked widespread fear, causing a sharp drop in market prices, with a fall of ten taels, resembling a rapid collapse, breaking through the 560-tael mark. With the subsequent improvement in exchange rates, buyers regained momentum, and the market stabilized. After a period of calm, the price surged upward, jumping over ten taels and breaking through the 70-tael barrier. In the later market, Fuchang, Wanxing, Shunli, and others aggressively bought, while Zhifeng, Yong Bingxing, and smaller investors sold. Exchange rates remained inactive due to Wednesday's holiday, and the gold price hovered around the 570-tael mark. The volatility of the market left participants disoriented.

After the opening, there was a sharp drop. Yesterday, the British pound had risen by sixteen points, and the silver price by a quarter. The opening price for July was 567.5 taels, an increase of eight qian. It then rose to 68 taels, with small investors buying in. Subsequently, a rush to sell by various firms led to a negative sentiment, causing a sharp drop of ten taels, ultimately falling to 57 taels and one qian. The initial assessment was that the market should be bullish. When more buying followed, the British pound rose by two or three points. When it opened at 57 taels and two qian, June British gold transactions between banks were at 7 pence 625. Then, British gold rose by half a penny, the U.S. dollar by one yuan, and Japanese gold fell by three and a half points. At that time, the gold price was still around 58 taels, which was mainly due to small transactions in the morning. Suddenly, there was a rush upward, as the foreign exchange market showed signs of tightening. August settlement was at 7 pence 625. Korean demand for July Japanese gold was 1 tael, 1 qian, 4 fen, 7.5. A grain merchant offered August at 7 pence 3225. As a result, the gold price surged, jumping up ten taels, reaching 67 taels by 10:30 AM, then falling back three or four taels, reaching 62 taels, three or four qian around 11:00 AM. Later, it rallied, with eager buyers, causing another surge of ten taels, albeit with fluctuations of one or two taels at times. By noon, it was at 72 taels, closing at 71 taels and eight qian.

The highest price in the later market reached 73 taels. The later market opened at 70 taels and 0.8 qian, then rose from 1 tael and 4 qian to 69 taels and 6 qian. Seeing strong buying, the price rose by more than three taels, reaching 73 taels. Subsequently, there was a sudden drop of four or five taels. Zhifeng Yong and others were selling. Around 2:30 PM, the price was at 67 taels and eight qian. Afterwards, the market gradually rallied, with Fuchang, Shunli, and Wanxing aggressively buying, leading to a steady rise. By 3:45 PM, it had broken through the 70-tael mark again. As the foreign exchange market was inactive, the price rose by five taels after 4:00 PM, reaching 572 taels and seven qian. There was a slight dip momentarily, and the market closed at 4:30 PM at 71 taels and six qian, an increase of 4 taels and nine qian compared to the 10th.

Small transactions amounted to forty or fifty taels. The largest price difference in one day was 73 taels, and the smallest was 57 taels and one qian, a difference of 15 taels and nine qian. The announced price was changed to 611 taels and four qian, a reduction of fifty taels, down to forty taels. In the afternoon, there was a reduction of forty taels. Registered account replenishment was at 72 taels. Physical goods opened at 67 taels and five qian in the morning, closing at 70 taels at noon, and closing in the afternoon at 70 taels and five qian.

The market was bustling with activity. Firms involved in transactions included Fuchang, Bingxing, Yuankangxiang, Wanxing, who were buying; Zhifeng Yong, Yu Da, Chengfeng Yong, Yong Chengchang, Xiangyu, Yuancheng, Yuanxing Yongfu Yu, who were selling. Taixing and Hengxing had fluctuating positions. In the afternoon, Fuchang, Wanxing, Shunli, Hengxing, and Yufa Yong were generally buying, while Dadecheng, Yuancheng, Yuanyu Yong, and Fuyu were generally selling. Firms were frequently buying and selling. The Dalian firms had a total of over 4,000 transactions in the morning, with balanced buying and selling after consolidation. In the later market, there were over 1,000 buying transactions and three or four hundred selling transactions. The Guangdong firms had a total of over 1,000 transactions.

Yesterday, HSBC foreign exchange rates continued to rise by two points, due to large transactions and rising silver prices. British gold rose by half a penny to 1 shilling and 7 pence 25. General Market Situation

Yesterday, although the silver interest rate market was robust, the lack of collateral among those in need was less severe than in previous days, with adequate funds available for withdrawals. (Silver Interest Rates)

Origins of the Downturn in Forward Flour 116

Bulls rushed to sell, and factories secretly unloaded.

Yesterday, the flour market experienced a period of sluggishness in the morning, down by about one fen compared to the previous day's closing. Subsequently, short covering revitalized the market, with near-term contracts rebounding by two fen and forward contracts rebounding by about one fen. When the market opened in the afternoon, the current month remained tight, reaching a high of 2 taels, 5 qian, 7 fen half. However, starting from July, as major bull positions rushed to sell, or had already entirely reversed course, factories also softened their stance and secretly unloaded forward contracts. As a result, buying momentum weakened, and the market showed signs of loosening.

Observation: As spot prices opened at 2 taels, 6 qian, 5 fen, the current month ultimately remained firm. With forward contracts considered to be far off, and factories continuing to unload, prices were likely to fluctuate. The current month rose by 2 li half compared to the previous day, while July fell by 7 li half, August fell by 1 fen, and September fell by 5 li. October and November fell by 7 li half.

Near-Term Wheat Surges Seven Fen 117

New wheat is being acquired by various factories, totaling 10,000 bags.

Yesterday, when the wheat futures market opened, prices for all months were generally flat and sluggish. However, subsequent trading saw an increase in momentum. Although the current month involved new wheat, recent deliveries to Shanghai were truly limited. The Jiangbei region would not begin full shipments until after the Grain in Ear festival. Furthermore, current inland prices were more expensive than the standard price. As a result, factories and industry insiders generally agreed to accumulate inventory, leading to aggressive price increases. Forward contracts also rebounded due to strong factory buying intentions. The market is expected to remain stable if inland prices do not decline.

The current month surged by seven fen compared to the previous day, August rose by three fen, September rose by four fen, and July, October, and November each rose by two fen. Factories are eager to acquire new wheat at high prices, with asking prices increasing by six to seven fen. Nanjing wheat: 4 taels 8 qian 7 fen. Kunshan wheat: 4 taels 9 qian 4 fen. Wusong wheat: 4 taels 8 qian 2 fen. Pudong wheat: 4 taels 7 qian 3 fen. Penglai Town wheat: 4 taels 9 qian 2 fen. Jiading wheat: 4 taels 8 qian 7 fen. A total of 10,000 bags were opened. Old wheat prices also increased by four fen due to depleted inventories. Xu Zhou and Bengbu wheat were quoted at 5 taels 2 qian half, totaling 2,000 bags.

Silk and Tea: Xiushui Black Tea Halted Due to Banditry 119

Xiushui and Wuning black tea markets had gradually improved this year, with dozens of firms setting up shops to procure tea. First-grade boxed teas were already packaged and awaiting shipment. However, on the 16th of last month, bandit Peng Dehuai invaded and captured the Xiushui county seat. Most of the tea shops in Baishang, west of the city, were burned down, and the tea stored in the shops was burned and looted, resulting in significant losses. The tea market was completely halted. Military forces were encircling and attacking, pushing them towards the Hunan border. However, the local losses were severe, and it is uncertain whether the tea shops can rebuild and resume operations.

Tunxi Tea Market Plummets 120

The high-grade Zhenmei tea from Tunxi tea firms that rushed to Shanghai failed to obtain favorable prices. Concerns are unusually high. No one inquired about the new tea arriving from various routes, and even tea from Wuyuan's high-quality farms was priced low. As of recently, Tunxi tea firms still had over 4,000 dan of unsold tea. High-quality tea was priced at 40 yuan, while lower-quality tea was only 20 yuan. The tea market is plummeting.

Transportation Issues for Wuyuan Boxed Tea 121

The first-grade Zhenmei teas from Wuyuan's various villages have been gradually boxed. Aside from the west route (Fuchun, Huchuan, Dayoushan), the north route (Fengshan, Hongguan Ridge Foot), the south route (Zhongyun, Kengtou Kongcun), and the east route (Daban, Jiangwan, Xitou) being exported via Jingde and Tunxi, the middle, lower, north, and city area boxed teas have relied on the Lehe waterway for transportation. However, the Lehe River has been blocked due to the rampant banditry. As a result, most of the boxed Zhenmei teas have been stockpiled in the shops and cannot be transported.

Yesterday, Zhangcun Jixianglong and other firms, seeking to avoid losses, hired porters to transport teas through the drought road to Shangxikou, and then via Tunxi and Hangzhou to Shanghai. Each porter carried six dan of boxed tea. Firms are now planning to transport tea through this route. However, as the farming season is in full swing, it is difficult to find so many porters. Thus, transporting boxed tea to Shanghai has become a major issue for the tea market. Firms are hesitant. The new tea markets in various villages have been affected by these issues, and prices have declined again. Yesterday, tea from Yanshan, Tuochuan, and Liyuan was priced from 54 yuan to 58 yuan, while tea from Zhuangtian and Shatan was priced at 51 yuan, 15 yuan lower than in mid-June. The remaining routes saw little trading, and the market was unusually quiet.

Foreign Firm Silk Market Remains Stagnant 122

The local foreign firm silk market is nearly collapsing. European sales remain stagnant. Although the silk exchange rate continued to rise yesterday, overseas silk prices were reported to be falling again. Shanghai's new silk telegrams did not indicate a rebound. Chinese silk merchants are losing too much due to the silk capital relationship, so it is difficult to sell at a lower price. The silk market is helpless, and manufacturers are unable to mediate.

疋頭元素府綢走銷大暢 123

Fine cloth and plain silk fabrics sold extremely well.

The cloth market recovered its calm, but prices rose too quickly, causing actual sales to hesitate. In addition, the money market was unusually tight, and those selling off goods also announced a halt. Yesterday, merchants in the eastern market subtly signaled movement, and a rebound is possible. White crepe and Yuan Yang yarn remained firm and expensive due to shortages. Yuan Zhi Gong Ni and Zhi Gong Duan gradually stabilized. There was an increasing amount of fine broadcloth in stock. Huxinting was priced at 2 qian 4 fen 7 li 5 hao, Lie Yan Mu Qiu at 2 qian 4 fen 2 li 5 hao, and Gucheng Hui at 2 qian 8 fen 5 hao, a drop of 2 li 5 hao from before. Hua Biao frequently appeared at new lows, having already fallen below the 3 liang 9 qian mark. The lesser quality patterns were only about 6 qian. The extreme cheapness of the price has never been seen before, so Shanghai goods have also slightly declined. Among Western goods, plain silk fabrics were the most popular. More than ten boxes a day were sold in the Xiaodongmen area, leading to a sharp rise in prices. De Ji Jin Gongzi was priced at 6 qian 7 fen 5 hao, Feng Yu Da Fugui at 6 qian 2 fen 5 hao, Kang Fu goods at 6 qian, and Li Xin goods at 5 qian 2 fen 5 hao, an increase of 1 qian to 5 fen.
