June 12th, 19th Year of the Republic of China (Shen Bao, This Green Garden

School Drama's

Selection of Scripts 204

The meaning and effectiveness of the school drama movement, simply put, is to make life dramatized. In our Chinese school life, everyone feels that it is too dull, dry, monotonous, and meaningless. The dead and heavy air pressure only sees the nation's one day of weakness and decline, or catches up with the road of depravity. Therefore, we have to borrow the power of literature and art as a material to awaken their will, excite and invigorate, recognize the bright road of life, strive to pursue the achievement of career, and destroy all the century's morbidities.

Since the new art form of drama has established its position in China, the school drama movement has had a special progress. In the past, it was a naive expression of emotional impulses in the style of civilized drama. Now it is a metaphysical improvement, a new artistic exploration of life. Especially in the past two years of development, we looked at the history of the school drama movement and it is worth our surprise. The drama clubs of various schools have sprung up like mushrooms after rain. Not only universities but also middle schools are organizing one after another. Female students have also liberated the dignity of the boudoir and sacrificed themselves to run to the palace of art together. Those who are capable hold public performances independently, and those who are weak participate in the recreational activities. We should pay considerable respect to their spirit and perseverance.

This is the investigation of facts, and the theoretical exploration and publicity are also quite effortful and cannot be erased. Therefore, we can know more that the school drama movement has deepened a stage and gained considerable praise in education. Originally, the power of drama is to give people strength, to give people education, to give people entertainment, and to give people the method of life. Youth is just a youth When the flower is blooming beautifully, we must make it perfect, stand at the forefront of the times, actively struggle forward, and use their enthusiasm and boiling blood in the right place. This is what drama wants to influence them. The steps of drama can be divided into three paragraphs: one is selecting scripts, two is rehearsing, and three is bringing it to the stage. Since our biggest object is to give young people the power of life, then the first step we need to pay attention to should be the script. The scripts we want to apply must absolutely avoid low-level tastes, old-fashioned patterns, and erroneous concepts of class meaning, and be suitable for how to give our nation a new life. In other words, what we require is how to make (the national consciousness) sound. With a good script, we can express a good play and give people a deep impression | sympathy and emotion, as if these things were my own experiences.

Now, although many drama groups in various schools understand it, there are also many who have not grasped the new art form of drama, and even fallen into the wrong path. We can know this by observing the scripts announced by the public performances of various drama groups. Of course, there is still a lack of good scripts in China, but there are also not a few good scripts translated from foreign countries. The biggest problem is that the value of drama is lost for the sake of propaganda of a certain kind of thought. I think it is very wrong. Therefore, I express a little opinion on the selection of scripts for school dramas.

(1) Drama occupies a great power in the national movement. It encourages the national spirit of independence. Now is the era when we are seeking national independence. In the past, our national spirit was too depressed. Now we must re-promote and invigorate it. In thoughts, emotions, interests, customs, human feelings, and environment, we must pay attention to not letting young people forget their future mission.

(2) It is to promote education and make them experience life and recognize the world. Use rich content to make them understand the various different appearances of life and the typicality of human nature. It is also to explain and guide, so that they forget the so-called difficulty and ease, do not make meaningless roars, do not make meaningless lamentations, and bravely stride forward on the bright road of walking upward.

This is the script required by school dramas. I hope that the students who are working hard in the school drama movement will jointly discuss and guide the selection of scripts for various school drama groups. This is a project that cannot be neglected. If our school drama develops universally (Li Chunsen)

Youth Garden Manuscript Rules 205

(1) The text is limited to discussions on youth issues, domestic and foreign school or student news, essays, descriptions of school life, essays, etc. The style is not limited. (2) Chinese paintings are limited to those related to youth issues. (3) Photos are limited to those that photograph youth life (such as sports, travel, tours, drama performances, speeches, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements. Both individuals and groups are welcome. (4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper. (5) The number of words in each article should not exceed two thousand. (6) Do not write the manuscript horizontally and do not write carelessly. Western texts can be omitted if possible. If it is necessary to cite the original text, it must be attached below the translation.
